    SELECT `x8`.`Id`
    FROM `Clients` AS `x8`
    WHERE `x8`.`ClientId` = @__clientId_0
    ORDER BY `x8`.`Id`
    LIMIT 1
) AS `t7` ON `x.Properties`.`ClientId` = `t7`.`Id`
ORDER BY `t7`.`Id`
